***ebben.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ebben.html>ebben</a> (83756)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ebben.html>ebben</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ebbon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*abjōną</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ebben.html>ebben</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ebb, to recede <span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">especially of tides</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">eben</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ebeen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hebenus</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a> (wood)</li></ol>

<p>From older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">ebenhout</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">ebenushout</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ebenus</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ebben.html>ebben</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hout.html>hout</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wood</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>The dark tropical wood <a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a> (83755)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3><p>
From earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">hebeny</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">ebenif</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">hebenyf</i> (influenced by <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hebeninus</i>), from Ecclesiastical <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ebenius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">of <a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">hebenus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ebon tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔβενος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ébenos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egyptian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Egyptian language">Egyptian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy">hbnj</i>, </p> </td></tr></tbody></table>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a></strong> (<i>usually uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">ebonies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A hard, dense, deep black wood from various subtropical and tropical trees, especially of the genus <i>Diospyros</i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A tree that yields such wood.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">countable and uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A deep, dark black colour.
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel"><a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>ebony</a> colour: <span style="background-color:162632; display:inline-block; width:80px;"> </span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A black key on a <a href = vnd.unilang:piano.html>piano</a> or other keyboard instrument.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1982</b>,  Paul McCartney (<a href = vnd.unilang:lyrics.html>lyrics</a> and music),  “Ebony and Ivory”, in  <cite>Tug of War</cite>, performed by Paul McCartney amp; Stevie Wonder:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ebony.html>Ebony</a></b> and ivory / Live together in <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> harmony / Side by side on my <a href = vnd.unilang:piano.html>piano</a> keyboard / <a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a> lord, why don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a>?</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***echt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> (92)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ēhaft</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*aiwahaftaz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective_2">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echter.html>echter</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">echtst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>authentic, true, genuine, real
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></span></span></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:onecht.html>onecht</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:nep.html>nep</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vals.html>vals</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<ol><li>really, truly</li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li>marriage, matrimony

***echtbreekster.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreekster.html>echtbreekster</a> (107252)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From echtbreken 'wreck a marriage, commit adultery' (from <a href = vnd.unilang:echt.html>echt</a> 'marriage' + <a href = vnd.unilang:breken.html>breken</a> 'to break [cognate], wreck')  + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ster</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreekster.html>echtbreekster</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreekster.html>echtbreeksters</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreekster.html>echtbreekstertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreker.html>echtbreker</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>An female adulterer, who <a href = vnd.unilang:breaks.html>breaks</a> his (or her) marital bond</li>
<li>A female homewrecker</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:overspelig.html>overspelige</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtbreuk.html>echtbreuk</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:echtgenote.html>echtgenote</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ijsbreker.html>ijsbreker</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm">eclipse</i>, ***economie.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a> (5404)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">oeconomia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἰκονομία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oikonomía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">management of a household, administration</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">οἶκος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oîkos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">νόμος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nómos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">law</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (surface analysis <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">eco-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-nomie</i>). The first recorded sense of the word <b><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></b>, found in a work possibly composed in 1440, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> “the management of economic affairs”, in this case, of a monastery.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economieën</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economietje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>economics</li>
<li>economy</li></ol>

***economisch.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:economisch.html>economisch</a> (18822)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:economie.html>economie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">economics, economy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-isch</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ish, -ic(<a href = vnd.unilang:al.html>al</a>)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>.
</p>

</p>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An eczema, geeric term for <a href = vnd.unilang:itchy.html>itchy</a> and/or defiguring inflammations of the skin</li>

***eddy.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a> (7855)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">edēa</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turning, back, reverse</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">ēa</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ed-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ea</i><sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A current of air or water running back, or in an opposite direction to the main current.
<ul><li><b>1922</b>, A. M. Chisholm, <i>A Thousand a Plate</i>
<dl><dd>In the bow old Dobbs fought the stream cunningly, twisting the nose into <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> and backwaters, taking advantage when he could of set of current, and when he could not, paddling doggedly, not so powerfully, perhaps, as his partner, but with equal steadiness.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A circular current; a whirlpool.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Dryden and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd>And smiling <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> dimpled on the main.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1713</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Joseph_Addison" class="extiw" title="w:Joseph Addison">Joseph Addison</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cato,_a_Tragedy" class="extiw" title="w:Cato, a Tragedy">Cato</a></cite>, published 1712, [Act 2, scene 6]:</span><dl><dd></dd></dl></div>
<dl><dd>Wheel through the air, in circling <b><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b> play.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="derivedterms CategoryTreeTag" data-ct-mode="10" data-ct-options="{quot;modequot;:10,quot;hideprefixquot;:20,quot;showcountquot;:false,quot;namespacesquot;:[0],quot;notranslationsquot;:false}"><div class="CategoryTreeSection"><div class="CategoryTreeItem"><span class="CategoryTreeBullet"><span class="CategoryTreeToggle" data-ct-title="English_words_prefixed_with_ed-" data-ct-state="collapsed">►</span> </span> English <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> prefixed with ed-</div><div class="CategoryTreeChildren" style="display:none"></div></div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:eddies.html>eddies</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">eddying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">eddied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To form an <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a>; to move in, or as if in, an <a href = vnd.unilang:eddy.html>eddy</a>; to move in a circle.
<ul><li><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(Can <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> date this quote by Wordsworth and provide title, author's full name, and other <a href = vnd.unilang:details.html>details</a>?)</span>
<dl><dd><b>Eddying</b> round and round they sink.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1922</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sinclair_Lewis" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Sinclair Lewis">Sinclair <a href = vnd.unilang:lewis.html>Lewis</a></a>,  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/en:Babbitt/Chapter_25" class="extiw" title="s:en:Babbitt/Chapter 25">Chapter 25</a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Babbitt" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Babbitt">Babbitt</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Neither in his voiceless cabin, fragrant with planks of new-cut pine, nor along the lake, nor in the sunset <a href = vnd.unilang:clouds.html>clouds</a> which presently <b>eddied</b> behind the lavender-misted mountains, could Babbitt find the spirit of Paul as a reassuring presence.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:edel.html>edel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">noble</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:metaal.html>metaal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">metal</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:ili.html>ili</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sole of the foot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eem.html>eem</a> (107228)</h1><br></body> 
***een.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> (9)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_4">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">êen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ein</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ainaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*óynos</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Article">Article</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong> (<i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">'n</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite article</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Placed before a singular noun, indicating a general case of a person or thing:</span> a, an. Compare with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></i>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_2">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>one</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<ul><li>When it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unclear from the context whether <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the number or the indefinite article, the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written with acute accents: <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">één</i>. In all other <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> written without. For example, <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 'one of those'. But <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i> can mean both 'one apple' and 'an apple', so if the former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> intended one would write <i><b>één</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:appel.html>appel</a></i>.</li></ul>
<dl><dt>Examples</dt></dl>
<ul><li><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a></i>: a hat; <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:oor.html>oor</a></i>; an ear.</li>
<li><i><b>Eén</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>allen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>allen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b>één</b></i>: one for all, all for one. (The <a href = vnd.unilang:motto.html>motto</a> of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Three_Musketeers" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Three Musketeers">The Three Musketeers</a>.)</li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> / <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>

***eend.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eend.html>eend</a> (5145)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:ent.html>ent</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eent</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">ened</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*anadz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂énh₂t-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:enten.html>Ente</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">ennet</i>. More at <span class="Latn" lang="en">ennet</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one, mono</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dek.html>dek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">deck, plane</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>, a loan translation of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">single decker</i>.

***eenheid.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a> (2379)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">eenheit</i>, likely calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">ūnitās</i>. Some modern senses likely derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Einheit</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-heid</i>, analogous to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">oneness</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheden.html>eenheden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenheid.html>eenheidje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>unity</li>
<li>unit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">measure</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military<span class="ib-comma">,</span> law enforcement</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unit <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">squad or party; member of a military organisation or law enforcement organisation; division</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> loneliness
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eenzaamheid.html>eenzaamheid</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:eentonig.html>eentonig</a> (35194)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">één</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-y, -ish</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eentonig.html>eentonig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eentonig.html>eentoniger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">eentonigst</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literally</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> monotonous (having an unvarying tone or pitch)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:monotone.html>monotone</a>, tedious(ly unvaried); boring, dull</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
